## Methodology
- For each word at level N, check all content words in its definition
- If a word in the definition is NOT in level в‰¤ N vocabulary в†’ it's "и¶…зєІ"
- Function words (117 common words) are excluded
- CRITICAL: в‰Ґ5 и¶…зєІиЇЌ, MAJOR: в‰Ґ3 и¶…зєІиЇЌ
